### [1] [PhysX-Omni: Unified Simulation-Ready Physical 3D Generation for Rigid, Deformable, and Articulated Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21572)
*Ziang Cao,Yinghao Liu,Haitian Li,Runmao Yao,Fangzhou Hong,Zhaoxi Chen,Liang Pan,Ziwei Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PhysX-Omni：一个统一的、面向多类型资产（刚体/可形变/关节体）的“可仿真”物理3D生成与理解框架；引入无压缩高分辨率几何表示、构建通用数据集PhysXVerse与评测基准PhysX-Bench（几何、绝对尺度、材质、可供性、运动学、功能描述），在传统指标与新基准上均表现优异，并展示在场景生成与机器人策略学习中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D生成方法要么忽视物理属性，要么只覆盖单一资产类型，难以直接用于物理仿真和具身智能下游任务。需要一个统一框架，既能生成高保真几何，又能携带物理属性并支持多类型资产，同时有通用数据与评测体系。

Method: 1) 设计面向多模态/视觉-语言模型的高效几何表示，直接编码高分辨率3D结构、无需压缩；2) 构建通用“可仿真”3D数据集PhysXVerse，覆盖室内外多类别与物理属性；3) 提出综合评测PhysX-Bench，涵盖几何、绝对尺度、材质、可供性、运动学、功能描述六大属性；4) 训练统一的PhysX-Omni模型，评估其生成与理解能力，并在场景生成与机器人策略学习中做应用验证。

Result: 在传统生成指标与PhysX-Bench上均取得强性能，相较现有方法在几何质量与物理相关属性（尺度、材质、可供性、运动学、功能）上明显提升；展示了端到端生成“可仿真”场景与支持机器人策略学习的可行性。

Conclusion: PhysX-Omni作为统一框架打通了多类型物理3D资产的生成与理解，借助新数据集与基准促进可仿真资产生态，预期将推动具身智能与物理仿真等广泛下游应用的发展。

Abstract: Simulation-ready physical 3D assets have emerged as a promising direction owing to their broad applicability in downstream tasks. However, most existing 3D generation methods either neglect physical properties or are limited to a single asset category, e.g., rigid, deformable, or articulated objects. To address these limitations, we introduce PhysX-Omni, a unified framework for simulation-ready physical 3D generation across diverse asset types. Specifically, we develop a novel and efficient geometry representation tailored for Vision-Language Models, which directly encodes high-resolution 3D structures without compression, significantly improving generation performance. In addition, we construct the first general simulation-ready 3D dataset, PhysXVerse, covering diverse indoor and outdoor categories. Furthermore, to comprehensively and flexibly evaluate both generative and understanding capabilities in the wild, we propose PhysX-Bench, which encompasses six key attributes: geometry, absolute scale, material, affordance, kinematics, and function description. Extensive experiments with conventional metrics and PhysX-Bench show that PhysX-Omni performs strongly in both generation and understanding. Moreover, additional studies further validate the potential of PhysX-Omni for applications in simulation-ready scene generation and robotic policy learning. We believe PhysX-Omni can significantly advance a wide range of downstream applications, particularly in embodied AI and physics-based simulation.

</details>


### [2] [Lens: Rethinking Training Efficiency for Foundational Text-to-Image Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21573)
*Dong Chen,Fangyun Wei,Ziyu Wan,Dongdong Chen,Jiawei Zhang,Jinjing Zhao,Sirui Zhang,Yang Yue,Zhiyang Liang,Baining Guo,Chong Luo,Jianmin Bao,Ji Li,Lei Shi,Qinhong Yang,Xiuyu Wu,Xuelu Feng,Yan Lu,Yanchen Dong,Yitong Wang,Yunuo Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Lens 是一款 3.8B 参数的文本到图像模型，在多项基准上达到或超过 >6B 模型的水平，同时仅用约 Z-Image 19.3% 的训练算力；通过高信息密度数据+多分辨率批训练、改进架构（语义VAE与强语言编码器）、以及RL与蒸馏加速，实现高质量、多语言与任意常见纵横比生成，并在H100上实现快速推理（1024² 3.15s，蒸馏版4步0.84s）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在T2I领域现有SOTA多依赖更大参数与更高算力，训练成本高、推理慢且对多语言与多纵横比泛化不足。作者希望在显著降低训练开销的同时，保持或超越SOTA质量与多样性，并提升收敛速度、分辨率/纵横比泛化、以及多语言可用性。

Method: 1) 数据与批次设计：使用Lens-800M（800M张图，GPT-4.1生成的密集长描述，平均约109词）；在每个batch中混合多分辨率与多纵横比图像以扩大全视觉覆盖。2) 架构：采用语义VAE以获取更优潜变量表示；使用更强语言编码器，加速优化并从仅英文数据实现多语言泛化。3) 训练后优化：用基于分类体系的提示集合（Lens-RL-8K）与结构化奖励进行RL抑制伪影、提升质量；引入reasoner模块并通过免训练的系统提示搜索改进对齐；蒸馏实现4步推理加速。

Result: 以3.8B参数在多项基准上与≥6B模型竞争并多处超越；仅用Z-Image约19.3%的训练算力即可达成；可从1:2到2:1任意纵横比、分辨率至1440²泛化；支持多种常用语言提示；单张1024²图在H100上3.15秒，蒸馏版4步0.84秒。

Conclusion: 通过高信息密度数据、批内多尺度/纵横比、语义VAE与强语言编码器、以及RL与蒸馏等系统优化，Lens在小参数规模下实现高效训练与高质量生成，并具备多语言与广覆盖纵横比的稳健泛化与快速推理。

Abstract: We introduce Lens, a 3.8B-parameter T2I model that achieves performance competitive with, and in several cases surpassing, state-of-the-art models with more than 6B parameters across various benchmarks, while requiring significantly less training compute. For example, Lens requires only about 19.3% of the training compute used by Z-Image. The training efficiency of Lens stems from two key strategies beyond its compact model size. First, we maximize data information density per training batch by (i) training on Lens-800M, a dataset of 800M densely captioned image-text pairs whose captions are generated by GPT-4.1 and contain approximately 109 words on average, providing richer semantic supervision than conventional short captions, and (ii) constructing each batch from images with multiple resolutions and diverse aspect ratios, thereby enlarging the effective visual coverage of each optimization step. Second, we improve convergence speed through careful architectural choices, including adopting a semantic VAE that provides better latent representations and employing a strong language encoder that accelerates optimization while enabling multilingual generalization from English-only training data. After pre-training, we apply RL with taxonomy-driven prompts (Lens-RL-8K) and structured reward rubrics to suppress artifacts and improve visual quality, a reasoner module with training-free system prompt search to better align user requests with the model, and distillation-based acceleration for 4-step inference. Through efficient training and systematic optimization, Lens generalizes to arbitrary aspect ratios from 1:2 to 2:1 and resolutions up to 1440^2, and supports prompts in several commonly used languages. Thanks to its compact size, Lens generates a 1024^2 image in 3.15 seconds on a single NVIDIA H100 GPU, while its distilled turbo version performs 4-step generation in 0.84 seconds.

</details>


### [3] [GenEvolve: Self-Evolving Image Generation Agents via Tool-Orchestrated Visual Experience Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21605)
*Sixiang Chen,Zhaohu Xing,Tian Ye,Xinyu Geng,Yunlong Lin,Jianyu Lai,Xuanhua He,Fuxiang Zhai,Jialin Gao,Lei Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GenEvolve提出一种“自进化”的图像生成智能体，通过工具编排的轨迹和视觉经验蒸馏，使模型在复杂、多样的生成请求中更好地检索证据、选参考、用技能、写提示，最终在多个基准上达到了SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放式图像生成日益复杂，单纯“提示到图像”难以满足高质量、多样化需求；现有代理式方法多依赖图像级标量奖励，难以提供细粒度监督，导致工具使用、检索与提示构造效率不佳。作者希望构建能跨任务有效用工具并可自我进化的通用图像生成代理。

Method: 提出GenEvolve框架：将每次生成视为“工具编排”的轨迹（收集证据、选择参考、调用生成技能、组合成prompt-reference程序）。比较同一请求下的多条轨迹，抽象出最佳与最差的差异，形成结构化的“视觉经验”，仅提供给教师分支；采用类似on-policy的自蒸馏，进行稠密token级监督，指导学生内化更优的搜索、知识激活、参考选择与提示构造。并构建GenEvolve-Data数据集与GenEvolve-Bench基准。

Result: 在公开基准与自建GenEvolve-Bench上显著优于强基线，达到当前图像生成框架的SOTA；表现出更强的工具使用与复杂任务适应能力。

Conclusion: 通过工具编排的轨迹比较与视觉经验蒸馏，GenEvolve实现了可自我进化的通用图像生成代理，解决了仅靠标量奖励监督不足的问题，带来细粒度学习信号与更高的生成质量与稳健性。

Abstract: Open-ended image generation is no longer a simple prompt-to-image problem. High-quality generation often requires an agent to combine a model's internal generative ability with external resources. As requests become more diverse and demanding, we aim to develop a general image-generation agent that can self-evolve through trajectories and use tools more effectively across varied generation challenges. To this end, we propose GenEvolve, a self-evolving framework based on Tool-Orchestrated Visual Experience Distillation. In GenEvolve, each generation attempt is modeled as a tool-orchestrated trajectory, where the agent gathers evidence, selects references, invokes generation skills, and composes them into a prompt-reference program. Unlike existing agentic generation methods that mainly rely on image-level scalar rewards, GenEvolve compares multiple trajectories for the same request and abstracts best-worst differences into structured visual experience, provided only to a privileged teacher branch. Inspired by on-policy self-distillation, Visual Experience Distillation provides dense token-level supervision, helping the student internalize better search, knowledge activation, reference selection, and prompt construction. We further construct GenEvolve-Data and GenEvolve-Bench. Experiments on public benchmarks and GenEvolve-Bench show substantial gains over strong baselines, achieving state-of-the-art performance among current image-generation frameworks. Our website is as follows: https://ephemeral182.github.io/GenEvolve/

</details>


### [4] [UniVL: Unified Vision-Language Embedding for Spatially Grounded Contextual Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21611)
*Jiayun Wang,Yu Wang,Weijie Gan,Zhenting Wang,Wei Wei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出UniVL用于空间定位的上下文图像生成，将文本指令直接渲染到空间掩码中作为统一视觉输入，去除独立文本编码器；在自建UniVL-ImgGen上显著提升图像质量并降低推理成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统可控生成通常分离图像与文本两个编码器，难以精确表达“什么在何处”的空间约束，且推理负担重（独立文本编码器开销大）。需要一种统一且高效的条件范式，将语义与空间位置紧密绑定并降低计算。

Method: 1) 任务：空间落地的上下文图像生成；用户把文字指令写在空间掩码上，与参考视觉内容一起形成单一视觉输入。2) 模型：UniVL编码器基于OCR预训练骨干，光学读取统一条件，输出融合视觉、语义与空间的token序列fVIL。3) 两阶段：先对齐UniVL与VAE嵌入空间；再用预训练扩散模型仅以UniVL嵌入为条件进行生成，移除如T5等文本编码器。4) 训练与数据：构建含477K掩码标注图像的UniVL-ImgGen用于训练/评测。5) 消融：验证各组件贡献。

Result: 在UniVL-ImgGen基准上，相比文本提示基线：FID从14降至11，PSNR从16升至20；完全去除文本编码器，使推理TFLOPs降低最多52%，运行时长缩短最多44%。

Conclusion: 统一条件范式将语义与空间位置在视觉域内直接绑定，既提升质量又显著降本，为高效、空间可控的图像生成提供了有效路径。

Abstract: We introduce spatially grounded contextual image generation, a controllable image generation task that reframes the conditioning paradigm. Instead of supplying a reference image and a global text prompt through two separate encoders, one for vision and one for language, UniVL is trained to bind semantics to spatial locations directly from a single unified visual input, where the textual instruction is rendered onto the spatial mask. This removes the need for a standalone text encoder at inference time. The resulting model supports contextual image generation by following user-specified instructions about what should appear where, while substantially reducing computation.
  To address this task, we propose a framework in which the UniVL encoder, adapted from an optical-character-recognition-pretrained backbone, reads the unified condition optically and produces a UniVL embedding, fVIL, that fuses visual and semantic intent with spatial locations in a single token sequence. A two-stage pipeline first aligns UniVL with the VAE embedding space and then conditions a pretrained diffusion backbone entirely on UniVL embeddings, eliminating the standalone text encoder, such as T5. Although this reframing uses a deliberately minimal text interface, it yields strong empirical gains. On UniVL-ImgGen, a benchmark of 477K mask-annotated images that we construct for training and evaluation, UniVL improves image quality over text-prompted baselines, reducing FID from 14 to 11 and increasing PSNR from 16 to 20. It also eliminates the text encoder entirely, reducing inference TFLOPs by up to 52% and runtime by up to 44%. Additional ablation studies validate the contributions of the proposed components, paving the way for efficient, spatially grounded image generation with a unified conditioning paradigm.

</details>


### [5] [Flat-Pack Bench: Evaluating Spatio-Temporal Understanding in Large Vision-Language Models through Furniture Assembly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21625)
*Aditya Chetan,Eric Cai,Peeyush Kushwaha,Bharath Raj Nagoor Kani,Utkarsh Mall,Qianqian Wang,Noah Snavely,Bharath Hariharan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Flat-Pack Bench基准，聚焦家具组装视频中的细粒度时空理解，发现现有LVLM在排序、定位、配合与跟踪等方面表现不佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频基准多为粗粒度任务（分类、检索、字幕等），且依赖易于语言识别的实体，难以评估现实复杂场景中对细粒度时空理解（如装配步骤、部件交互、接触关系、跟踪）的需求。

Method: 构建以家具组装为核心的新基准Flat-Pack Bench，通过带视觉提示（高亮相关部件）的多选题评估LVLM在四类细粒度任务上的能力：1）装配动作的时间顺序判断；2）装配状态的时间定位；3）部件配合/接触关系理解；4）部件跟踪。以多模型实验衡量性能。

Result: 多种主流/最先进LVLM在该基准上显著失分，暴露出难以有效利用视频时序信息、跟踪能力不足、以及对空间交互（如物理接触）理解薄弱等问题。

Conclusion: 细粒度时空推理仍是LVLM的短板；Flat-Pack Bench为系统评测此类能力提供了新测试场，指向需改进的方向：更强的时序建模、鲁棒跟踪与物理交互理解。

Abstract: The emergence of Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) has significantly advanced video understanding capabilities. However, existing benchmarks focus predominantly on coarse-grained tasks such as action segmentation, classification, captioning, and retrieval. Furthermore, these benchmarks often rely on entities that can be easily identified verbally, like household objects, animals, human subjects, etc., limiting their applicability to complex, in-the-wild video scenarios. But, many applications such as furniture assembly, cooking, etc., require step-by-step fine-grained spatio-temporal understanding of the video, which is not sufficiently evaluated in current benchmarks. To address this gap, we introduce Flat-Pack Bench, a novel benchmark centered on furniture assembly tasks. Our benchmark evaluates LVLMs on nuanced tasks, including temporal ordering of assembly actions, temporal localization of assembly state, understanding part mating, and tracking, using multiple-choice questions paired with visual prompts highlighting relevant parts as references for fine-grained questions. Our experiments reveal that state-of-the-art LVLMs struggle significantly with fine-grained spatio-temporal reasoning, highlighting their limitations in effectively leveraging temporal information from videos, limited tracking ability, and understanding of spatial interactions like physical contact.

</details>


### [6] [Ablate-to-Validate: Are Vision-Language Models Really Using Continuous Thought Tokens?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21642)
*Tianyi Zhang,Mahtab Bigverdi,Ranjay Krishna*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出并验证一种诊断原则“删改以证（Ablate-to-Validate）”，用标准化的“Token Replacement Test (TRT)”来判断视觉-语言模型中的连续/潜在非文本token是否被真正用于推理。结果显示：即使篡改或替换这些token的内容，多数精度提升仍然保留，说明很多所谓“视觉思维”收益并非源自token内容本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大量VLM用连续或潜在的“思维”token来提升视觉推理，但仅凭准确率提升无法证明模型真的利用了这些token进行推理，可能只是上下文长度、特殊token锚定或训练正则等混杂因素造成。需要一个能分离“token存在”与“token内容”作用的诊断方法。

Method: 提出Ablate-to-Validate原则，并具体化为TRT：在保持提示、图像、token预算与解码策略固定的条件下，将中间潜在token替换为零向量、随机向量、首次重复（first-repeat）或“oracle”替代，观察性能变化，从而辨别性能是否依赖token内容。作为可控试验，作者在相对深度推理任务上，训练LLaVA-13B与Qwen2.5-VL-3B去预测并消耗连续或离散的深度span，覆盖多种冻结视觉编码器（SigLIP2、CLIP、DINOv2）与token预算；并将TRT应用到Mirage、Mull-Tokens、CoVT等现成系统，在BLINK、VSP、CV-Bench上评测。

Result: 在所有设置下，即使将潜在token内容破坏或替换，模型的大部分性能增益仍然存在。由此表明：准确率提升常常是误导性的代理指标；模型往往并未将潜在通道当作信息瓶颈来实际使用。

Conclusion: 应将TRT与准确率并列为引入连续“思维token”方法的标准诊断工具。仅靠准确率不足以证明“视觉思维”token被用于推理，社区需要采用内容删改对照来验证机制性利用。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are increasingly augmented with continuous or latent non-textual tokens intended to support "visual thinking." Despite improved task accuracy, this alone does not show that models actually use these tokens for reasoning -- gains may arise from confounds such as added context length, special-token anchoring, or training-time regularization. We formalize a diagnostic principle, Ablate-to-Validate, for testing whether latent-token content is genuinely utilized, and instantiate it as the Token Replacement Test (TRT), a standardized suite of content-replacement ablations. TRT holds the prompt, image, token budget, and decoding fixed while replacing intermediate tokens with zero, random, first-repeat, or oracle alternatives, isolating whether performance depends on token content or merely on token presence. As a controlled testbed, we study relative depth reasoning with LLaVA-13B and Qwen2.5-VL-3B, training models to predict and consume continuous or discrete depth spans across multiple frozen encoders (SigLIP2, CLIP, DINOv2) and token budgets. We additionally apply TRT to three off-the-shelf visual-thinking systems (Mirage, Mull-Tokens, CoVT) on BLINK, VSP, and CV-Bench. Across all settings, accuracy gains are a misleading proxy for latent-token reasoning: VLMs retain most improvement even when token content is corrupted or replaced, revealing a persistent gap between having a latent channel and using it as an information bottleneck. We recommend TRT as a standard diagnostic alongside accuracy for any method introducing continuous thought tokens.

</details>


### [7] [Look-Closer-Then-Diagnose: Confidence-Aware Ultrasound VQA via Active Zooming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21652)
*Yue Zhou,Erxuan Wu,Yikang Sun,Hongjoo Lee,Yuan Bi,Huixiong Xu,Zhongliang Jiang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出用于超声VQA的“先放大再诊断”与不确定性感知奖励的框架，显著提升病灶定位（+39.3%）并在模糊情形更谨慎。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有通用/医学VLM在超声任务表现不佳：未显式模拟临床中“先关注病灶区域再给出诊断”的交互式观察流程；且把标注当作无偏真值，忽视超声判读的主观性与模糊性，导致在不确定样本上自信过度、推理不聚焦。

Method: 1) 结构化的Zoom-then-Diagnose范式：模型先交互式搜索并放大可疑病灶，再基于局部与全局信息进行问答/诊断，实现病灶聚焦推理。2) 在GRPO（Group Relative Policy Optimization）框架下引入不确定性感知奖励：通过随机的分组rollouts估计预测一致性，作为模型置信度代理；据此对清晰样本强化正确预测，对模糊样本抑制过度自信。

Result: 在肝、乳腺、甲状腺多套数据上验证：病灶定位性能提升39.3%；同时展现出主动放大查看并诊断的能力，整体VQA性能与稳健性提升（文中重点报告定位与一致性收益）。

Conclusion: 将临床声科医师的“先看病灶后诊断”认知流程与不确定性建模纳入VLM训练，可在超声VQA中实现更精确的定位与更稳健的决策，对含主观性与歧义的医学影像任务具有推广价值。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have significantly advanced medical visual question answering, yet their performance in ultrasound remains suboptimal. In clinical practice, sonographers explicitly focus on lesion regions to formulate reports, though diagnostic interpretations sometimes vary due to inherent subjectivity. However, existing VLMs are not explicitly structured to interactively zoom into lesions prior to diagnosis; moreover, they typically treat annotations as unbiased ground truths, failing to account for their inherent subjectivity and ambiguity. In this paper, we propose a framework specifically designed to consider the sonographer's cognitive workflow. We first introduce a structured Zoom-then-Diagnose paradigm, which replicates the interactive search process to enable lesion-focused reasoning. Furthermore, within the Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) framework, we introduce an uncertainty-aware reward derived from stochastic group-wise rollouts to estimate prediction consistency as a proxy for model confidence. Together, these two components encourage the model to reinforce accurate predictions on clear cases while remaining cautious under ambiguity. Experiments across liver, breast, and thyroid datasets show that our framework improves lesion localization by 39.3\%, demonstrating that our model has learned the ability to actively look closer and diagnose.

</details>


### [8] [MRecover: A Conditional Generative Model for Recovering Motion-Corrupted MR images Using AI Generated Contrast](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21669)

Abstract: Hippocampal subfield segmentation requires high-resolution T2w turbo spin echo (TSE) MRI, yet this sequence is susceptible to motion artifacts, leading to substantial data loss. The synthesized images also achieved larger effect sizes due to increasing the sample size for diagnostic group differences in hippocampal subfield atrophy (whole hippocampus $ε^2$= 0.121-0.100 vs. 0.086-0.062, left-right hemispheres). ### [9] [AVI-HT: Adaptive Vision-IMU Fusion for 3D Hand Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21714)
*Ziyi Kou,Ankit Kumar,Mia Huang,Taylor Niehues,Vatsal Mehta,Ergys Ristani,Li Guan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AVI-HT提出一种自适应视觉-IMU融合的手部3D姿态追踪框架，通过头戴/自体视角图像与手套上6DoF IMU的联合建模，在重遮挡HOI场景显著提升精度与可用性；基于配准的多模态训练数据与跨传感器注意力机制实现对视觉与各IMU信号的动态信任分配，在DexGloveHOI数据集上相较多种基线平均关键点误差降低16.1%，腕对齐变体降24.2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于视觉的手部追踪在手物交互中易受遮挡、运动模糊与视角变化影响而失效；纯IMU方法缺乏全局几何约束易漂移。需要一种能在不同观测质量下自适应融合多源传感的方案，以提升鲁棒性与精度，并量化IMU在不同手指/活动中的贡献与对噪声、对齐误差的敏感性。

Method: 1) 采集同步多模态训练数据：自体视角相机与手套上多颗6DoF IMU，同时由动捕系统提供3D手部关键点真值，构成DexGloveHOI（>10万对齐样本，涵盖多物体日常任务）。2) 设计跨传感深度注意力机制：学习在时间上和传感器维度上对视觉特征与各指IMU特征进行自适应加权，按场景质量动态调节信任度。3) 在两种手部模型设定（UmeTrack与MANO）下训练与评测，并进行消融分析（逐指IMU贡献、噪声与时序失配敏感性）。

Result: 与多种单/多模态基线相比，AVI-HT平均关键点误差降低16.1%，腕对齐变体降低24.2%；在强遮挡HOI场景可靠性更高。消融表明各手指IMU对性能提升的差异性显著，且模型对IMU噪声与视觉-IMU时间错位具有一定敏感度但总体可控。

Conclusion: 通过配准的视觉-IMU数据与跨传感注意力，AVI-HT在复杂HOI中实现更稳健、更精确的3D手势追踪；IMU传感器提供对遮挡的关键补充，注意力机制实现对多源质量的动态适配。数据集与分析为后续在噪声鲁棒与时序对齐上的改进提供了依据。

Abstract: We present AVI-HT, an adaptive visual-IMU fusion approach for tracking 3D hand poses by jointly modeling the egocentric image with on-glove 6-DoF IMU signals. AVI-HT achieves significantly improved accuracy and availability, particularly in hand-object interaction (HOI) scenarios involving heavy visual occlusion. Two complementary ingredients underpin its success: (1) synchronized multi-modal training data pairing on-body vision-IMU sensor streams with ground-truth 3D hand poses from a motion-capture system, and (2) a cross-sensor deep attention mechanism that adaptively modulates the trust assigned to the vision and individual IMU sensors. To evaluate AVI-HT in real-world settings, we conduct extensive experiments on our DexGloveHOI dataset that consists of 100K+ pairwise vision-IMU samples with synchronized 3D annotated poses, in which users manipulate a variety of objects during daily tasks. We compare against multiple single- and multi-modal tracking approaches under two hand models (UmeTrack, MANO). The results show that AVI-HT reduces mean keypoint error by 16.1% and its wrist-aligned variant by 24.2% over the baselines. Ablation studies further reveal the per-finger contribution of IMU sensors across activity types, and the model's sensitivity to IMU noise and temporal misalignment in vision-IMU fusion.

Abstract: Image captioning evaluation remains a significant challenge, as vision-language models evolve toward more challenging capabilities such as generating long-form and context-rich descriptions. State-of-the-art evaluation metrics involve extensive computational costs associated with the use of Large Language Models (LLMs) as judges, or instead suffer from the limitations of standard CLIP-based encoders, such as strict token limits, lack of fine-grained sensitivity, or lack of compositional generalization by treating captions as ``bags-of-words.'' Our training scheme uses a carefully assembled data mixture for supervised learning, featuring adversarial LLM-based data augmentations to enhance model sensitivity to fine-grained visual-linguistic errors. We also introduce a new benchmark designed to assess detailed captioning evaluation across diverse scenarios. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed metric achieves state-of-the-art performance while maintaining the efficiency required for large-scale benchmarking, quality-aware decoding, or reward guidance.

### [12] [BodyReLux: Temporally Consistent Full-Body Video Relighting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21766)
*Li Ma,Mingming He,Xueming Yu,David M. George,Ahmet Levent Taşel,Paul Debevec,Julien Philip*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 采集：结合静态OLAT与新型动态交替光序（两段平滑变化光序快速交织，高于人眼融合阈值避免闪烁），获得像素对齐的重光照视频对；2) 模型：以预训练文本到视频扩散模型为基底迁移训练；3) 条件：将每个光源表示为“令牌”，并通过掩码注意力对光序列进行条件化，实现动态光照控制；4) 数据增强：专门设计的增强流程提升鲁棒性与时序一致性。

Abstract: Being able to relight human performance is a fundamental task for post production and content creation. We present BodyReLux, a subject-specific video diffusion-based framework for relighting full-body human performances in a temporally consistent way. Our model is trained on a hybrid dataset of pixel-aligned video relighting pairs, covering a diverse combination of lighting conditions, performances and viewpoints. To acquire such dataset, we combine traditional static One-Light-at-a-Time (OLAT) capture and a novel dynamic performance capture in which two smoothly varying lighting sequences are rapidly interleaved. Because the lighting operates above the human flicker-fusion threshold, the interleaving does not appear to strobe. We train our video relighting model from a pretrained text-to-video model to fully leverage the generative priors for producing high quality videos. To achieve accurate lighting control, we introduce a new lighting conditioning method that represents each light source as a token. We further condition on sequences of lighting using masked attention to support dynamic lighting control. Together with a carefully designed data augmentation pipeline, we achieve photorealistic, robust, and temporally consistent video relighting of subject-specific human performances.

Main category: cs.CV

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 用RGB-D多视角重建场景并生成3D场景图，显式编码物体的语义与空间关系；2) 设计“视觉标记提示”策略，使VLM从2D视图中推断物体-物体关系；3) 将2D关系提升到持久的3D场景图；4) 将自然语言查询解析为查询图；5) 在约束条件下对查询图与场景图进行图匹配与对齐，确保多视角一致性与可解释推理。

Abstract: Zero-shot 3D visual grounding requires localizing objects in unstructured environments from free-form natural language. Recent vision-language model (VLM) approaches achieve promising results but rely on view-dependent reasoning or implicit representations, limiting spatial consistency and interpretability for compositional queries. We propose SceneGraphGrounder, a framework that reformulates 3D grounding as structured graph matching over a reconstructed 3D scene graph. To enable this formulation, we introduce a visual marker prompting strategy that enables a VLM to infer object-object relationships from 2D views, which are subsequently lifted into a persistent 3D scene graph encoding both spatial and semantic relations. Given a query, we construct a query graph and perform constrained alignment with the scene graph, ensuring multi-view consistency and interpretable reasoning. Experiments on the ScanRefer benchmark demonstrate that our method achieves competitive performance among zero-shot approaches, using only RGB-D inputs. We further validate our framework through real-world deployment on a mobile robot, demonstrating robust spatial reasoning in long-horizon physical environments. We will make our code publicly available upon acceptance.

We address this gap by introducing (1) a benchmark for referential communication in dynamic 3D environments, built from 6.7 hours of egocentric VR interaction with synchronized speech, motion, gaze, and 3D scene geometry, and (2) a two-stage grounding pipeline that explicitly resolves conversational ambiguity before visual localization. The benchmark includes over 4,200 manually verified referring expressions spanning full, partitive, and pronominal types. Our contextual rewriting approach improves grounding performance by 11-22 percentage points on average, with a pure detector (GroundingDINO) reaching 56.7% on pronominals after rewriting, nearly double the best end-to-end baseline.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 构建Seizure-Semiology-Suite：438视频、>35k密集标签、覆盖20个ILAE半定量学特征；2) 设计7项分层基准，从低级视觉感知到时间排序、叙述性报告生成与诊断；3) 提出报告质量指标Seizure-RQI用于临床意义评估；4) 在11个开源MLLM上做基线；5) 进行癫痫领域特定微调；6) 设计两阶段神经-符号框架用于分类。

Result: 基线显示MLLM在偏侧性推理、时间定位、症状时序和临床忠实报告方面存在系统性弱点；领域微调显著提升所有任务表现；两阶段神经-符号方法在癫痫与非癫痫分类上达F1=0.96。

Conclusion: Seizure-Semiology-Suite为安全关键医疗视频理解提供严格基准与评测工具，揭示现有MLLM不足并指引构建临床可靠、可适配领域的多模态智能。

Abstract: While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated remarkable proficiency in general video understanding, their capacity to interpret involuntary, and spatio-temporally evolving pathologic motor behaviors such as seizure semiology remains largely untested. To address this gap, we introduce Seizure-Semiology-Suite, a clinically grounded dataset and benchmark for fine-grained, structured seizure semiology understanding. The dataset includes 438 seizure videos annotated with over 35,000 dense labels covering 20 ILAE-defined semiological features. Building on this dataset, we propose a seven-task hierarchical benchmark that systematically evaluates MLLMs from low-level visual perception to temporal sequencing, narrative report generation, and seizure diagnosis. To enable clinically meaningful evaluation of generated reports, we further introduce the Report Quality Index for Seizure Semiology (Seizure-RQI). Extensive baselines across 11 open-weight MLLMs reveal systematic weaknesses in laterality reasoning, temporal localization, symptom sequencing, and clinically faithful reporting. We show that seizure-specific fine-tuning substantially improves performance across tasks, and that a two-stage neuro-symbolic framework achieves an F1 score of 0.96 on epileptic versus non-epileptic seizure classification. Seizure-Semiology-Suite establishes a rigorous benchmark for evaluating multimodal models in safety-critical medical video understanding and guides the development of clinically reliable, domain-adaptive multimodal intelligence.

### [16] [CrossVLA: Cross-Paradigm Post-Training and Inference Optimization for Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21854)
*Zhi Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文研究跨范式VLA（自回归离散token vs 连续动作流匹配）在偏好对齐中的统一DPO后训练，并报告显著性能与效率结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DPO在语言模型中是事实标准，但在VLA里主要用于离散自回归架构；连续动作的流匹配模型因缺少对数概率而难以直接用DPO。需要一个统一方法比较不同范式并评估参数高效调优与推理效率瓶颈。

Method: 提出用于连续动作流匹配模型的替代性log-prob估计器，使DPO无需概率流ODE积分即可作用于flow-matching骨干；系统比较LoRA与DoRA作为VLA DPO的参数高效适配层；进行推理时间剖析（去噪循环与缓存策略），并预训练多视角+时序投影头以实现同任务帧检索。

Result: 在LIBERO四套基准（600次试验、3个seed）上，DoRA+DPO较OpenVLA的SFT平均提升+10.4个百分点：各子套件分别+20.0（Object）、+11.0（Long-horizon）、+8.0（Goal）、+2.7（Spatial），且Object子集三个seed均38/50（方差为0）。推理端，去噪循环占78.6%动作采样延迟；前缀K/V缓存（VLA-Cache风格）理论加速上限约21%，分块/逐token缓存在其基准中成功率下降至0–80%。多视角+时序投影在6000帧上实现同任务检索k-NN recall@1为99.5%（较随机提升36倍）。

Conclusion: 提出的log-prob替代估计使DPO可跨范式用于连续动作VLA；DoRA优于LoRA并带来稳定增益；VLA推理主要瓶颈在去噪循环，缓存带来的加速有限且可能伤害成功率；提供高质量多视角时序初始化与完整开源资源。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have rapidly converged on a small set of architectural patterns: discrete-token autoregression (e.g. OpenVLA) and continuous-action flow-matching (e.g. pi-0.5). Yet preference alignment via Direct Preference Optimisation (DPO) -- the de-facto post-training step in language models -- has been studied almost exclusively on autoregressive VLAs. We present CrossVLA, an empirical study of cross-paradigm VLA post-training. Three contributions: (i) a surrogate flow-matching log-probability estimator that lets DPO operate on continuous-action backbones without probability-flow ODE integration; (ii) a head-to-head comparison of LoRA and DoRA as the parameter-efficient layer for VLA DPO, finding DoRA improves over OpenVLA SFT by a mean +10.4 pp across LIBERO 4-suite (600 trials, 3 seeds) -- per-suite +20.0 Object, +11.0 Long-horizon, +8.0 Goal, +2.7 Spatial -- with zero seed variance on Object (38/50 on each of 3 seeds); (iii) an inference-time anatomy showing the denoise loop dominates 78.6% of sample_actions latency and prefix-K/V caching a la VLA-Cache caps at a 21% acceleration ceiling -- both chunk-level and token-level cache strategies degrade success rate to 0-80% in our benchmarks. We further pretrain a multi-view + temporal projection head on 6000 LIBERO frames, achieving 99.5% k-NN recall@1 for same-task retrieval (36x over random), available as a downstream initialisation. All code, ckpts, training logs, and reproduction scripts are open at https://github.com/lz-googlefycy/vla-lab.

Method: 提出Director-Experts (DEX) 模块化架构：每个堆叠模块含专家池与导演两部分。专家池通过“逐图像激活策略”动态选择/调度专家，使其自发专长于不同模态主导统计；导演通过“组指数滑动平均(EMA)”聚合多专家知识，蒸馏到共享表示空间以促进跨模态语义对齐。基于4M图像/10模态的新基座数据集Medical Vision Universe进行FM级预训练，并在多任务上评测。

Abstract: Multi-modality medical vision (MV) foundation models (FM) are fundamentally challenged by pronounced Non-IID feature statistics across heterogeneous imaging modalities. Monolithic self-supervised optimization on such data induces conflicting gradients, driving representations to collapse toward modality-dominant shortcuts. This work reframes this failure as an imbalance between specialization and coordination in emergent modularity, and proposes Director-Experts (DEX), a modular network that explicitly regulates these dynamics in stacked modules. Each DEX module comprises a pool of experts, dynamically adapted by our image-wise activation strategy, autonomously specializing in modality-dominant statistics, together with a director, updated via our group exponential moving average, which distills multi-expert knowledge into a shared space for semantic integration across modalities, thus driving the emergence of modular representations. We curate a new benchmark, Medical Vision Universe, over 4 million images across 10 modalities, which provides a FM-level pre-training with the broadest coverage of distinct imaging modalities to our DEX. Extensive evaluations on 26 downstream tasks demonstrate improved optimization behavior and transferability, indicating DEX as a principled step toward general-purpose multi-modality medical AI. Our code and dataset will be opened at https://github.com/YutingHe-list/DEX.

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) often fail under low illumination because their visual grounding is learned predominantly from RGB imagery, whereas thermal infrared preserves complementary scene structure when visible cues degrade. We present Thermo-VL, a wavelength-aware VLM that augments a frozen Molmo-7B backbone with a trainable thermal encoder and a text-guided dual-attention fusion module. Given aligned RGB tokens, thermal tokens, and prompt embeddings, the fusion module conditions thermal features on both language and RGB context, then injects a gated residual into the frozen RGB stream so thermal evidence can be incorporated without disrupting Molmo's pretrained RGB-language interface. We train the model with the standard language-modeling objective together with auxiliary alignment and regularization losses that improve cross-modal grounding and reduce over-reliance on RGB. We also introduce a pixel-aligned RGB-thermal instruction-tuning dataset and Thermo-VL-Bench, a manually screened RGB-thermal VQA benchmark for low-light and cross-spectrum reasoning. Experiments show strong gains on challenging thermal-only and RGB+thermal reasoning tasks, highlighting the value of prompt-conditioned multispectral fusion. Our dataset and code are publicly available at: https://thusharakart.github.io/Thermo-VL

Here we present FlexiCT, a family of CT foundation models trained by agglomerative continual pretraining on 266,227 CT volumes from 56 publicly available datasets, forming a large-scale public resource for CT representation learning. FlexiCT uses agglomerative pretraining across three stages: two-dimensional axial pretraining, three-dimensional anatomical pretraining and report-guided semantic alignment. *Gang Dai,Yining Huang,Yiming Xia,Guohao Chen,Shuaicheng Niu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出RTS：在扩散模型推理阶段进行奖励引导和稀疏化的轨迹缩放，以超越静态噪声池TTS方法，显著提升生成质量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 奖励引导的噪声优化：在推理过程中依据外部或学习到的奖励信号，主动更新噪声方向以朝“高回报”区域搜索；2) 稀疏TTS框架+PCA曲率分析：对去噪全轨迹进行主成分/曲率评估，选择关键中间步进行重点搜索与优化，从而压缩搜索空间并分配更多预算于高影响步骤。

Abstract: The efficient Test-Time Scaling (TTS) paradigm offers a promising perspective for enhancing the generation performance of diffusion models. However, current solutions are limited to a static, pre-defined noise pool and suffer from inflexible noise exploration across the denoising trajectory. To bridge this gap, we propose RTS, a novel Reward-guided Trajectory Scaling method to fully unlock the generative potential of diffusion models. Unlike existing methods, RTS facilitates the synthesis of refined, high-fidelity images via two core innovations: 1) a reward-guided noise optimization strategy to actively direct the search towards promising regions; and 2) a sparse test-time scaling framework together with a PCA-driven curvature analysis scheme to prioritize key intermediate steps in the entire denoising space, effectively compressing the search space. To address this issue, we propose a novel multi-scale interaction network for stereo image super-resolution. Specifically, we design a Multi-scale Spatial-Channel Attention Module that utilizes multi-scale large separable kernel attention and simple channel attention to improve intra-view feature extraction. Additionally, we propose a Dual-View Epipolar Attention Module, utilizing an optimal transport algorithm to achieve more accurate matching along the epipolar line. Extensive experimental and ablation studies show that our method achieves competitive results that outperform most SOTA methods.

*Han Zhang,Wanting Jiang,Tomasz Kornuta,Tian Zheng,Vidya Murali*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MAVEN 是一个面向视频事件推理的数据构建与自适应标注流水线：以“焦点事件”为中心，从原始视频经多层描述（MSTED）生成多任务问答与CoT，并通过层级化自我诊断与重写持续提升数据质量；在交通监控等场景上为中等规模VLM微调带来显著增益，超过多款强基线并可快速迁移到新域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频事件推理需要高质量、结构化且可解释（含时间、空间、因果、后果等）的监督信号，而人工大规模标注成本高且难以覆盖多任务、多域需求。现有自动化方法缺少统一中间表示、弱于跨域自适应与错误溯源修正能力。

Method: 提出多阶段代理式标注流水线 MAVEN：1）从视频生成三层互补字幕，综合为多尺度时空事件描述 MSTED，围绕焦点事件组织；2）以 MSTED 为唯一输入，生成多任务Q&A与CoT；3）代理驱动的域自适应：根据新数据集与目标问题样例，自顶向下重设全部提示词与任务设计；4）层级化精炼循环：基于错误分类与溯源，定点重写提示或调整流水线结构，迭代提升质量。

Result: 对5300+交通监控视频标注并微调 Cosmos-Reason2-8B：在私有CCTV集上超越 Gemini 2.5 Pro 与 3.1 Flash，MCQ 比零样本提升+38.8 点；在 AccidentBench 上仅用 CCTV 训练即提升+10.7 点并追平 Gemini 2.5 Pro；加入代理适配的行车记录仪数据后逼近 Gemini 3.1 Flash；再经RL后训整体超越两款 Gemini 基线；在仓库安防与公共安全视频上展示可迁移性。

Conclusion: MAVEN 用显式中间表示与代理式自适应/自我修复闭环，系统性提升视频事件推理数据的质量与任务覆盖度，能高效迁移到新域并显著增强中等规模VLM的推理与问答性能。

Abstract: Training Vision Language Models (VLMs) for video event reasoning requires high-quality structured annotations capturing not only what happened, but when, where, why, and with what consequence, at a scale manual labelling cannot support. We present MAVEN (Multi-stage Agentic Video Event aNnotation), a multi-stage agentic pipeline that turns raw videos into multi-task training data with Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning traces, organized around a designated Event of Focus. At its core, MAVEN synthesizes a Multi-Scale Spatio-Temporal Event Description (MSTED) from three complementary caption levels; this explicit intermediate serves as the sole input to downstream Q&A generation across multiple task formats. Crucially, MAVEN supports agent-driven domain adaptation: given a new video dataset and target question examples, the agent redesigns all prompts top-down without manual re-engineering. A hierarchical refinement loop further classifies annotation errors against a taxonomy, traces root causes to the originating pipeline stage, and applies targeted edits that rewrite prompts or modify the pipeline structure itself, iteratively improving data quality. We apply MAVEN to label over 5,300 traffic videos and fine-tune Cosmos-Reason2-8B on the resulting data. On a private CCTV evaluation set, fine-tuning surpasses both Gemini 2.5 Pro and 3.1 Flash, including a $+38.8$-point gain in MCQ accuracy over zero-shot. On AccidentBench, CCTV-only training lifts Cosmos-Reason2 by $+10.7$ MCQ points and matches Gemini 2.5 Pro despite seeing no dashcam videos; adding agent-adapted dashcam annotations narrows the gap to Gemini 3.1 Flash, and RL post-training pushes overall performance past both Gemini baselines. Qualitative results on warehouse surveillance and public safety videos further show the agentic workflow readily adapts the pipeline to new domains.

</details>


### [24] [SDGBiasBench: Benchmarking and Mitigating Vision--Language Models' Biases in Sustainable Development Goals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21919)
*Zihang Lin,Huaiyuan Qin,Muli Yang,Hongyuan Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SDGBiasBench提出一个评估VLM在可持续发展目标（SDGs）场景中的系统性偏置的大规模基准，并给出一个训练-free的去偏集成方法CADE，显著提升选择题与回归任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SDG监测需要多模态推理（视觉、上下文、指标）并兼顾定性判断与定量估计，但现有基准往往分割评测，难以揭示模型以先验替代证据的系统性偏差；需要一个统一框架来全面测量决策级与估计级偏置并推动更公平可靠的AI。

Method: 构建SDGBiasBench：包含约50万条专家参与的多选题与5万条回归任务，覆盖SDG相关视觉-语言推理，专门设计以暴露模型依赖先验而非证据的偏置；并提出CADE（Contrastive Adaptive Debias Ensemble），一种训练-free、即插即用的集成方法，利用模态特定的答案先验进行对比式自适应加权以减轻偏置。

Result: 在SDGBiasBench上，现有VLM表现出内在SDG偏置（预测常受SDG特定先验驱动）；应用CADE在多模型上带来显著改进：多选准确率最高提升约25个百分点，回归任务的MAE最高降低约12点。

Conclusion: SDGBiasBench揭示并量化了VLM在SDG推理中的系统性偏置；CADE作为无需训练的去偏方案能有效缓解该问题。该工作为构建更公平、可靠的可持续发展AI系统提供了评测基准与实用方法。

Abstract: Assessing progress toward the Sustainable Development Goals (SDGs) requires multi-step reasoning over visual cues, contextual knowledge, and development indicators, where incomplete evidence use and imperfect evidence integration can introduce hidden prediction biases. Real-world SDG monitoring further spans both qualitative judgments and quantitative estimation. However, existing benchmarks typically evaluate these aspects in isolation, obscuring systematic biases that emerge when models substitute priors for evidence. To address this gap, we propose SDGBiasBench, a large-scale benchmark suite for SDG-oriented vision-language reasoning. Spanning 500k expert-involved multiple-choice questions and 50k regression tasks, the benchmark enables comprehensive assessment of both decision-level and estimation-level bias in Vision--Language Models (VLMs). Evaluations on SDGBiasBench reveal an intrinsic SDG bias in current VLMs, where predictions are frequently driven by SDG specific priors rather than reliable multi-modal cues. To mitigate such bias, we propose CADE (Contrastive Adaptive Debias Ensemble), a training-free, plug-and-play method that leverages modality-specific answer priors. CADE yields significant gains on the proposed benchmark, improving multiple-choice accuracy by up to 25% and reducing regression MAE by up to 12 points across multiple VLMs. We hope our work can foster the development of more fair and reliable AI systems for sustainable development.

### [25] [Visual-Advantage On-Policy Distillation for Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21924)
*Ruiqi Liu,Xiaolei Lv,Gengsheng Li,Ximo Zhu,Zhiheng Wang,Zhengbo Zhang,Junkai Chen,Zhiheng Li,Bo Li,Jun Gao,Shu Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VA-OPD：在视觉语言模型上进行“视觉优势”引导的在策略蒸馏，通过识别对细粒度视觉信息最敏感的高VA标记并区别化处理，显著提升学生模型的视觉依赖与下游表现，且随教师规模与数据规模单调增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统在策略蒸馏在VLM上虽能提升输出质量，但难以让学生真正“看图”：对于依赖细节的视觉关键词，学生对有/无细粒度视觉输入几乎不变，而教师强依赖视觉。这表明语言支架令视觉监督被稀释，需要一种能显式放大视觉监督信号的方法。

Method: 提出视觉优势VA：当教师对学生生成的序列打分时，比较教师在有与无细粒度视觉细节两种条件下的token级对数概率差；发现VA集中在少数token并代表视觉监督信号。基于此提出VA-OPD：1) 按“轨迹平均VA”对rollout级样本重加权；2) 将token按VA高/低分组，分别计算并平均组内KL，使高VA标记获得更大监督，避免被大量语言token稀释。方法在Qwen3-VL家族上跨3个教师规模进行。

Result: 在两组数学数据（Geometry3K、ViRL39K）训练，在八个数学推理与视觉理解基准上评测；与标准在策略蒸馏相比，VA-OPD在所有基准均提升，且增益随教师规模（4B→8B→32B）与数据规模增加而单调扩大。

Conclusion: 识别并放大“视觉优势”高敏感token，能在在策略蒸馏中更有效传递视觉监督，使学生更依赖视觉并获得一致的性能提升；教师更强与数据更多能与该策略正交叠加，带来更大收益。

Abstract: On-policy knowledge distillation has proven effective for language models, yet its application to vision-language models (VLMs) remains underexplored. We observe that standard on-policy distillation can improve a student's output quality while failing to strengthen its reliance on visual input: on vision-critical tokens, the student's predictions remain largely unchanged whether or not fine-grained visual detail is present, even though the teacher's predictions depend heavily on it.To make this difference observable, we introduce visual advantage (VA), the token-level log-probability difference when the teacher scores a student-generated rollout with versus without access to fine-grained visual detail. VA is concentrated in a small minority of tokens, and these high-VA tokens are the ones that actually carry the visual supervision signal. This motivates a distillation objective that treats them differently from language scaffolding, so their contribution is not diluted by the abundant surrounding language tokens.We propose Visual-Advantage On-Policy Distillation (VA-OPD), which uses VA at two granularities: rollout-level reweighting by trajectory-averaged VA, and token-level KL averaged within high-VA and low-VA groups separately. We train on two math datasets (Geometry3K and ViRL39K) and evaluate on eight benchmarks covering both mathematical reasoning and visual understanding, across three teacher sizes (4B, 8B, and 32B) on the Qwen3-VL family. VA-OPD improves over standard on-policy distillation on every benchmark, with the gain growing monotonically along both the teacher-size and data-scale axes, suggesting that these factors compound consistently.

### [26] [EvoVid: Temporal-Centric Self-Evolution for Video Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21931)
*Shiqi Huang,Ziyue Wang,Zhongrong Zuo,Han Qiu,Qi She,Bihan Wen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EvoVid提出一种无需标注、面向时间维度的自进化框架，让Video-LLM直接从原始视频中通过自博弈学习，显著提升跨多基座与多基准的时序推理能力，效果接近监督方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有用RL强化Video-LLM依赖人工构造任务与答案，成本高且受限于人类知识；已有自进化多为静态模态（文本/图像），无法刻画视频的时间动态，亟需能从未标注视频中自动挖掘时序监督的方案。

Method: 提出EvoVid，自博弈的Questioner-Solver框架，但面向视频的时间特性设计两类奖励：1) 时间感知Questioner奖励：通过对视频进行时间扰动并衡量问答敏感度，鼓励生成依赖时间顺序/持续性的高质量问题；2) 时间定位Solver奖励：让解答过程内生地进行视频片段定位，把正确答案与对应时间段对齐，形成自动化时序监督。系统在原始未标注视频上迭代优化。

Result: 在四个不同基座模型与六个基准上均取得一致提升，优于现有自进化基线，并达到接近或具竞争力的监督学习水平。

Conclusion: 时间中心的自进化范式能在无需人工标注的情况下有效提升视频理解与推理，是可扩展且高效的Video-LLM训练路径。

Abstract: Recent Video Large Language Models (Video-LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities in video reasoning through reinforcement learning (RL). However, existing RL pipelines rely heavily on human-annotated tasks and solutions, making them costly to scale and fundamentally constrained by human expertise. Self-evolving frameworks have recently emerged as a promising alternative through autonomous Questioner-Solver self-play. Unfortunately, these approaches are primarily designed for static modalities such as text and images, fundamentally failing to capture the temporal dynamics that are central to video reasoning. In this work, we propose $\textbf{EvoVid}$, a temporal-centric self-evolving framework that enables Video-LLMs to improve directly from raw, unannotated videos. Specifically, we introduce two complementary temporal-centric rewards: a temporal-aware Questioner reward that encourages temporally dependent question generation through temporal perturbation sensitivity, and a temporal-grounded Solver reward that provides automatic temporal supervision via inherent video segment localization. Extensive experiments across four base models and six benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements over both base models and existing self-evolving baselines, achieving competitive performance with supervised methods. These results highlight temporal-centric self-evolution as an effective and scalable paradigm for video understanding and reasoning.

### [27] [MLLMs Know When Before Speaking: Revealing and Recovering Temporal Grounding via Attention Cues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21954)
*Dazhao Du,Liao Duan,Jian Liu,Tao Han,Yujia Zhang,Eric Liu,Xi Chen,Song Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种推理时“先读后再生”的框架，利用MLLM预填阶段的跨模态注意力中隐藏的时间定位信号（TG-Heads），先定位高相关时间段，再以裁剪/掩码限制视觉上下文，从而无需训练即可显著提升视频时间定位性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前多模态大模型能流畅描述视频，但对事件起止时间的预测不可靠；已有方法要么依赖昂贵的时间标注微调，要么是粗糙的免训练启发式。作者发现模型在预填阶段其实已“知晓”目标时间区间，但在自回归生成答案时该信号被稀释转移，存在感知-生成鸿沟，促使其设计仅在推理时纠偏的方案。

Method: 1) 探测MLLM跨模态注意力，发现少数注意力头（TG-Heads）在预填阶段将查询到视频的注意力聚焦于真实时间区间；2) 将这些头的注意力转化为去偏的逐帧相关性信号并提取高注意区间；3) 再次调用同一MLLM，将视频上下文限制在该区间（通过视频裁剪或注意力掩码）以压制无关片段干扰；全程无需参数更新或模型结构改动。

Result: 在三大VTG基准上，对MiMo-VL-7B、Qwen3-VL-8B、TimeLens-8B均有稳定提升，最高提升达+3.5 mIoU；说明方法通用、有效且推理成本低。

Conclusion: MLLM在预填阶段蕴含可靠的时间定位线索，但在生成时被干扰；通过读（提取TG-Heads信号）后再生（限制视觉上下文）即可在零改参、零再训练下显著提升时间定位，缩小感知-生成鸿沟。

Abstract: Video temporal grounding (VTG), which localizes the start and end times of a queried event in an untrimmed video, is a key test of whether multimodal large language models (MLLMs) understand not only what happens but also when it happens. Although modern MLLMs describe video content fluently, their timestamp predictions remain unreliable, while existing remedies either require costly post-training on temporal annotations or rely on coarse training-free heuristics. In this work, we probe the cross-modal attention of MLLMs and uncover a perception-generation gap. Our key finding is that MLLMs often know the target interval during prefill, but lose this signal when generating the final answer. In the prefill stage, a sparse set of attention heads, which we call \emph{Temporal Grounding Heads} (TG-Heads), concentrates query-to-video attention on the ground-truth interval. During autoregressive decoding, however, the answer tokens shift attention away from this interval toward visually salient but query-irrelevant segments. This observation motivates an inference-time read-then-regenerate framework. We first convert TG-Head prefill attention into a debiased frame-level relevance signal and extract the high-attention interval it highlights. We then re-invoke the MLLM with visual context restricted to this interval, using video cropping or attention masking to suppress distractors. Without parameter updates and architectural changes, our framework consistently improves MiMo-VL-7B, Qwen3-VL-8B, and TimeLens-8B on three VTG benchmarks, with gains of up to +3.5 mIoU. The project website can be found at https://ddz16.github.io/mllmsknowwhen.github.io/.

</details>


### [28] [Bounding-Box Trajectories Matter for Video Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21957)
*Inpyo Song,Jangwon Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出TrajVAD：用归一化流建模多类别目标框轨迹的VAD框架；仅用轨迹即超越各姿态法（ShanghaiTech AP 87.7%，MSAD最佳）；加入姿态进一步到AUROC 88.6%、AP 90.9%。结论：目标框轨迹是被低估但高效的异常线索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人群场景中异常多与人相关，姿态法对外观鲁棒、运动表征紧凑，但普遍忽略在同一管线中天然可得的检测框轨迹；作者希望验证并系统化利用这一被忽视的强信号。

Method: 提出TrajVAD：用正态化流（normalizing flows）建模多类别目标框轨迹的正常运动学分布。两种变体：TrajVAD-T仅用边界框轨迹学习正常轨迹并据此检测异常；TrajVAD-P在此基础上融合姿态信息以进一步提升。

Result: 在ShanghaiTech上，轨迹-only的TrajVAD-T即超过所有姿态基线（AP 87.7%），并在MSAD上取得最佳；扩展版TrajVAD-P融合姿态后在ShanghaiTech达到AUROC 88.6%、AP 90.9%。

Conclusion: 边界框轨迹作为独立模态对视频异常检测极为有效且此前未被充分利用；以归一化流学习正常运动学可显著提升性能，姿态信息可在其上进一步增益。

Abstract: Video anomaly detection is critical for public safety and security, yet remains highly challenging despite extensive research due to large variations in appearance, viewpoint, and scene dynamics. Among existing approaches, human pose-based methods have emerged as a major line of research, showing strong performance since many anomalies in public datasets involve humans and pose representations are robust to appearance changes while providing compact motion descriptions. However, these methods often overlook bounding-box trajectories, although such information is inherently available in pose-based pipelines. In this paper, we explicitly leverage these trajectories as a primary anomaly cue. We present TrajVAD, a framework that models multi-class bounding-box trajectories using normalizing flows to learn normal kinematic patterns. Its trajectory-only variant (TrajVAD-T) eliminates pose estimation and surpasses all compared pose-based methods on ShanghaiTech in AP (87.7%), while achieving the best results on MSAD. An extended version (TrajVAD-P) incorporates pose information and further improves performance to 88.6% AUROC and 90.9% AP on ShanghaiTech, highlighting bounding-box trajectories as an effective yet underexplored modality for video anomaly detection.

### [29] [Dual-Integrated Low-Latency Single-Lens Infrared Computational Imaging for Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21964)
*Xuquan Wang,Guishuo Yang,Dapeng Yan,Yujie Xing,Xuanyu Qian,Kai Zhang,Xiong Dun,Jiande Sun,Zhanshan Wang,Xinbin Cheng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PDI-Net，将红外重建与目标检测深度耦合并嵌入光学先验，实现低延迟实时检测；在M3FD低信噪下，较剪枝的“重建+检测”方案推理提速84%，mAP@0.5:0.95提升5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算成像采用“重建→检测”的深度学习流水线带来较大延迟；多数加速只压缩重建网络，未充分利用成像光路的物理先验，导致精度-速度权衡。需要一个既快又准、能利用光学先验的端到端方案。

Method: 提出Physics-aware Dual-Integrated Network (PDI-Net)。训练阶段用监督式U-Net学习重建特征；推理阶段改为半U-Net编码器，特征直接共享给基于YOLO的检测器，避免完整图像重建。为衔接重建与检测特征，设计PALS-Bridge，利用视场相关的点扩散函数(PSF)先验，自适应调制多尺度卷积分支；并构建物理信息驱动的光学退化仿真用于训练与验证。系统部署在单镜红外相机上。

Result: 在M3FD基准的低SNR条件下，相较剪枝的“重建+检测”(Rec+Det)策略，推理时间降低84.06%，mAP@0.5:0.95提高5.07%；硬件上以单镜头替代多镜头，整机约减重50%。

Conclusion: 将光学物理先验融入重建-检测一体化网络，可在资源受限平台实现紧凑、低时延的红外实时检测，兼顾速度与精度，并具备工程落地潜力。

Abstract: Computational imaging enables compact infrared systems, but deep-learning pipelines that combine image reconstruction and object detection often introduce substantial inference latency. Most existing acceleration strategies compress the reconstruction network while overlooking physical priors from the optical path, leaving a trade-off between accuracy and speed. We present Physics-aware Dual-Integrated Network (PDI-Net), a low-latency framework that integrates infrared reconstruction with object detection and further embeds optical priors into the learning process. PDI-Net uses a supervised U-Net during training, while a semi-U-Net encoder shares features directly with a YOLO-based detector during inference, avoiding full image reconstruction. To bridge the gap between fidelity-oriented reconstruction features and detection-oriented semantics, we introduce a physics-aware large-small bridge (PALS-Bridge), which uses field-dependent point spread function priors to adaptively modulate multiscale convolutional branches. A physics-informed optical degradation simulation pipeline is also developed for training and validation. The method is deployed on a single-lens infrared camera, reducing system weight by about 50% compared with traditional multi-lens designs. On the M3FD benchmark under low-SNR conditions, PDI-Net reduces inference time by 84.06% compared with the Rec+Det with pruning strategy while improving mAP@0.5:0.95 by 5.07%. These results demonstrate compact, low-latency computational infrared imaging for real-time object detection on resource-constrained platforms.

### [30] [Foresee-to-Ground: From Predictive Temporal Perception to Evidence-Driven Reasoning for Video Temporal Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21973)
*Zelin Zheng,Xinyan Liu,Ruixin Li,Antoni B. Chan,Guorong Li,Qingming Huang,Laiyun Qing*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出F2G框架，将视频时序定位从“直接回归时间戳”改为“先识别再度量”，通过可验证的证据单元稳定边界预测并提升精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Video-LLM做VTG多基于从无结构视觉token直接生成时间戳，数值脆弱、边界不一致且难以验证。需要一种既稳健又可解释/可验证的时序定位方法。

Method: 提出Foresee-to-Ground (F2G)：1) 预测式时序感知，学习对边界敏感的时间表示，生成全视频候选事件片段，构成“证据池”；2) 证据驱动推理，将这些候选作为可引用的证据单元暴露给LLM，先进行事件识别（绑定显式事件假设），再进行边界测量，从而把“识别”和“精测”解耦，实现可验证定位。支持跨不同Video-LLM后端。

Result: 在多种基准上持续提升VTG定位准确率，能稳健迁移到不同的Video-LLM骨干，同时保持通用视频理解能力。

Conclusion: 将VTG重构为“识别-后-测量”的可验证流程，通过证据单元绑定事件与边界，显著稳定与提升时序定位性能并具备良好泛化。

Abstract: Current Video-LLM approaches for Video Temporal Grounding (VTG) typically rely on direct timestamp generation from an unstructured visual-token stream, often leading to brittle numerics and inconsistent boundaries. To address this, we propose Foresee-to-Ground (F2G), a framework that reformulates VTG as a verifiable Identify-then-Measure problem. F2G integrates Predictive Temporal Perception with Evidence-Driven Reasoning: it learns boundary-sensitive temporal representations to build a video-wide evidence pool of candidate event segments, and exposes these segments to the LLM as citable evidence units that bind boundary prediction to explicit event hypotheses. By decoupling event identification from precise boundary measurement, F2G stabilizes grounding and makes predictions verifiable. Extensive experiments demonstrate that F2G consistently improves grounding accuracy across diverse benchmarks, transfers robustly across different Video-LLM backbones, and preserves general video understanding capabilities.

</details>


### [31] [Video as Natural Augmentation: Towards Unified AI-Generated Image and Video Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21977)
*Zhengcen Li,Chenyang Jiang,Liangxu Su,Tong Shao,Shiyang Zhou,Ming Tao,Jingyong Su*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AIGC图像检测器在视频帧上普遍失效。论文诊断成因（视频处理带来的合成无关偏移+视频生成器指纹），并提出VINA：把视频帧当作“自然增强”，联合图像与视频训练并用跨模态监督式对比学习对齐表示，显著提升跨源/跨模态/部署鲁棒性并达SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AIGC检测器在训练/评测数据分布变化时易掉点，尤其从静态图像迁移到视频帧时性能崩溃。应用中内容来源多样（多数据源、编解码与处理链不同、图像/视频模态并存），迫切需要能在分布漂移和跨模态下稳健泛化的检测器。

Method: 提出VINA统一检测框架：1) 训练时同时使用图像与视频帧；2) 将视频预处理链（颜色空间转换、编码压缩、缩放、模糊等）视作“物理落地”的自然增强，从而学习对这些合成无关偏移的不变性；3) 设计跨模态监督式对比损失，促使图像与视频在共享的真/假判别边界下对齐表征；无需复杂手工增强或数据集特定调参。

Result: 在14个图像、视频及野外基准上，VINA实现双向增益（图像↔视频迁移互惠）、更强鲁棒性与可迁移性，并在几乎所有设置下达到SOTA。对比SOTA图像检测器在视频帧上“坍塌”的现象，VINA显著缓解该跨模态性能落差。

Conclusion: 跨模态泛化失败的根源既有视频处理链带来的分布偏移，也有视频生成器特指纹。通过把视频当作自然增强并用跨模态对比对齐，可以以统一方式训练出对图像与视频均稳健的AIGC检测器，实证上广泛SOTA且无需复杂特定调参。

Abstract: AI-generated content (AIGC) is rapidly improving, creating an urgent need for detectors that generalize across data sources, deployment pipelines, and visual modalities. A strongly generalizable detector should remain robust under distributional variations. However, we identify a consistent failure mode: SOTA AI-generated image detectors often collapse when applied to frames extracted from videos. Through systematic analysis, we show that this cross-modal gap arises from both entangled synthesis-agnostic video processing shifts, including color conversion, codec compression, resizing, and blur, and model-specific fingerprints introduced by modern video generators. Motivated by these findings, we propose VINA (Video as Natural Augmentation), a unified AIGC detection framework that jointly trains on image and video data. VINA uses video frames as physically grounded natural augmentations and further introduces a cross-modal supervised contrastive objective to align image and video representations under a shared real/fake decision boundary. Extensive experiments on 14 image, video, and in-the-wild benchmarks show that VINA delivers bidirectional gains, improves robustness and transferability, and achieves state-of-the-art performance across nearly all evaluated settings without complex augmentation or dataset-specific tuning.

### [32] [Interpreting and Enhancing Emotional Circuits in Large Vision-Language Models via Cross-Modal Information Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21980)
*Chengsheng Zhang,Chenghao Sun,Zhining Xie,Xinmei Tian*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种基于“引导向量（steering vector）”的因果归因框架，揭示并可在推理时操控LVLM对情绪的加工路径，从而在MER-UniBench上减缓情绪幻觉并提升情绪理解与叙述性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LVLM在情绪理解与共情生成方面表现突出，但我们缺乏对其内部如何把抽象视觉情绪线索转化为连贯叙事的机制性理解。现有难点在于：视觉反事实数据稀缺、情绪表达分散且语义弥散，导致因果分析与回路定位困难。作者希望提供可解释、可操控的情绪推理机制刻画与干预方法。

Method: 1) 提出面向描述性情绪推理的“引导向量”因果归因框架，定位与操控模型中的情绪回路；2) 构建专门数据集，刻画并验证“三阶段 Adapt–Aggregate–Execute”机制；3) 通过注意力与表征分析发现中层存在情绪特定（sentiment-specific）的注意力头用于聚合视觉情绪线索；深层通过情绪通用（emotion-general）通路将其转译为语言叙事；4) 基于上述洞见，设计推理时干预：调控情绪信息路由、增强注意力流、放大量化语义激活，以巩固情绪表达。

Conclusion: LVLM的情绪处理存在功能解耦：中层以情绪类内特异注意头聚合视觉情绪线索，深层以情绪通用路径生成语言叙事。基于引导向量的因果归因与路由调控可在推理阶段有效提升情绪相关性能并降低幻觉，提供理解与操控LVLM情绪推理的新范式。

Abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) represent a significant leap towards empathetic agents, demonstrating remarkable capabilities in emotion understanding. However, the internal mechanisms governing how LVLMs translate abstract visual stimuli into coherent emotional narratives remain largely unexplored, primarily due to the scarcity of visual counterfactuals and the diffuse nature of emotional expression. In this paper, we bridge this gap by introducing a steering-vector-based causal attribution framework tailored for descriptive emotional reasoning. To this end, we construct a specialized dataset to demystify the emotional circuits underlying the three-stage ``Adapt-Aggregate-Execute'' mechanism. Crucially, we discover a functional decoupling: visual emotional cues are aggregated in middle layers via sentiment-specific attention heads, but are subsequently translated into narrative generation in deep layers through emotion-general pathways. Guided by these insights, we regulate the emotional information routing to strengthen attention flow and amplify the semantic activation to consolidate expression. Extensive experiments on the comprehensive MER-UniBench demonstrate that our methods significantly improve performance via inference-time intervention, effectively mitigating emotional hallucinations and corroborating the causal fidelity of the discovered circuits.

### [33] [RiT: Vanilla Diffusion Transformers Suffice in Representation Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21981)
*Le Zhang,Ning Mang,Aishwarya Agrawal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出在预训练表征空间（特别是DINOv2特征）中用x-prediction的flow matching训练扩散式Transformer（RiT），显著提升采样质量与效率：ImageNet 256^2 上无引导FID 1.45、CFG后1.14，少参数且少步数（5–10步）即可达低FID。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管像素空间的x-prediction能很好利用低维流形，但像素分布存在协方差病态、厚尾与插值误差等问题，影响回归稳定性与收敛。作者猜想：若在预训练表征空间（保持相近内在维度）训练，或可获得更良性的统计几何性质，从而使flow matching更易学习、无需复杂头或黎曼传输。

Method: 系统比较像素、SD-VAE潜变量、DINOv2特征的四个几何统计轴：内在维度、有效秩、协方差条件数与超额峰度，以及流形内插误差。发现DINOv2与像素有相当内在维度（≈33），但在其余统计上显著更优；SD-VAE居中。基于此提出RiT：在冻结的DINOv2特征上，以x-prediction训练一个标准Diffusion Transformer，配合维度感知噪声日程与联合[CLS]-patch建模，无需特殊预测头或黎曼传输。

Result: DINOv2特征相较像素：有效秩高7.3倍，协方差条件数改善35倍，超额峰度降低11.5倍，流形内插误差降低1.7倍。ImageNet 256×256上：RiT无引导FID 1.45；采用CFG后1.14；优于DiT^DH-XL且参数少19%（676M vs 839M）。ODE求解粗步长即高质：CFG下5步Heun达FID 2.0，10步达1.25；无需蒸馏或一致性训练。

Conclusion: 预训练表征（尤其DINOv2）在保持数据流形内在维度的同时，显著改善分布的数值与几何条件，使flow matching的x-prediction回归更稳、更易优化。由此可用几乎“原味”的Transformer与简单训练策略实现更高质量与更高采样效率的生成；优势来自表征学习而非单纯压缩。

Abstract: Flow matching with $x$-prediction -- regressing the clean data point rather than the ambient velocity -- is known to exploit low-dimensional manifold structure effectively in pixel space \cite{li2025back}. We ask whether a pretrained representation space, while containing a low-dimensional data manifold of comparable intrinsic dimensionality, offers a distribution more favorable for flow-matching learning. Comparing pixel, SD-VAE, and DINOv2 features along four geometric axes, we find that pixel and DINOv2 share nearly identical intrinsic dimensionalities (both $\hat{d}\!\approx\!33$) yet DINOv2 exhibits $7.3\times$ higher effective rank, $35\times$ better covariance conditioning, $11.5\times$ lower excess kurtosis, and $1.7\times$ lower on-manifold interpolation error; SD-VAE latents are consistently intermediate, indicating that the advantage stems from representation-learning objectives rather than mere compression. These statistical properties render the flow-matching regression well-conditioned and remove the need for the specialized prediction heads or Riemannian transport used by prior DINOv2 diffusion methods. We propose the \emph{Representation Image Transformer} (RiT): a vanilla Diffusion Transformer trained by $x$-prediction on frozen DINOv2 features, augmented only by a dimension-aware noise schedule and joint \texttt{[CLS]}-patch modeling. On ImageNet $256{\times}256$, RiT attains FID 1.45 without guidance and 1.14 with classifier-free guidance, outperforming DiT$^\text{DH}$-XL with $19\%$ fewer parameters (676M vs.\ 839M). The resulting ODE is efficiently solvable at coarse discretizations: with classifier-free guidance, $5$ Heun steps already reach FID 2.0 and $10$ steps reach 1.25, without distillation or consistency training. Code at https://github.com/lezhang7/RiT.

</details>


### [34] [Learning Spatiotemporal Sensitivity in Video LLMs via Counterfactual Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21988)
*Dazhao Du,Jian Liu,Jialong Qin,Tao Han,Bohai Gu,Fangqi Zhu,Yujia Zhang,Eric Liu,Xi Chen,Song Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CRPO，一种在视频LLM上利用对照-反事实分支与奖励来抑制单帧/语言捷径、提升时空敏感性的RL框架；并发布DyBench用于严格评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频LLM常凭静态线索或语言先验答题，缺乏对时空动态的真正跟踪；传统基于“正确即奖励”的RL会进一步固化这种捷径。需要一种机制区分问题应随视觉动态而变或不变，从而约束策略学习真实时空关系。

Method: 提出CRPO：在训练中构造反事实视频（水平翻转、时间反转），建立原始与反事实的双分支RL；引入Counterfactual Relation Reward（CRR），根据问题类型（动态/静态）约束两分支答案的一致性或差异性，使仅依赖捷径的策略难以在两分支同时获高奖赏；并发布成对反事实基准DyBench与严格配对准确率P-Acc指标。

Result: 在Qwen3-VL-8B等模型上，CRPO在时空敏感评测上显著优于以往RL方法，同时保持通用视频任务性能：DyBench配对准确率提升+7.7，TimeBlind I-Acc提升+8.2，相比基线更少依赖静态捷径。

Conclusion: 通过反事实双分支训练与跨分支关系奖励，CRPO有效提升视频LLM对时空动态的敏感性并抑制捷径策略；DyBench提供客观评估。方法在不牺牲通用性能下带来稳健提升。

Abstract: Video large language models (Video LLMs) achieve strong benchmark accuracy, yet often answer video questions through shortcuts such as single-frame cues and language priors rather than by tracking spatiotemporal dynamics. This issue is exacerbated in RL post-training, where correctness-only rewards can further reinforce shortcut policies that obtain high reward without tracking video dynamics. We address this by asking a controlled counterfactual question: if the visual world changed while the question remained fixed, should the answer change or stay the same? Based on this view, we propose \textbf{Counterfactual Relational Policy Optimization (CRPO)}, a dual-branch RL framework for improving \emph{spatiotemporal sensitivity}. CRPO constructs counterfactual videos through horizontal flips and temporal reversals, trains on both original and counterfactual branches, and introduces a \textbf{Counterfactual Relation Reward (CRR)} between their answers. CRR encourages answers to change for dynamic questions and remain unchanged for static questions. This cross-branch constraint makes it difficult for shortcut policies to be consistently rewarded across both branches. To evaluate this property, we introduce \textbf{DyBench}, a paired counterfactual video benchmark with 3,014 videos covering reversible dynamics, moving direction, and event sequence, together with a strict pair-accuracy metric that prevents fixed-answer shortcuts from inflating scores. Experiments show that CRPO outperforms prior RL methods on spatiotemporal-sensitive evaluations while maintaining competitive general video performance. On Qwen3-VL-8B, CRPO improves DyBench P-Acc by +7.7 and TimeBlind I-Acc by +8.2 over the base model, indicating improved spatiotemporal sensitivity rather than stronger reliance on static shortcuts. The project website can be found at https://ddz16.github.io/crpo.github.io/ .

</details>

However, translating BIT volumes into clinically interpretable H&E images remains challenging, particularly due to shift-variant contrast and the absence of quantitative validation benchmarks. We introduce HistoBIT3D, the first voxel-wise paired BIT and fluorescence-labeled nuclei dataset, enabling quantitative evaluation of structural preservation in unsupervised virtual staining against ground-truth nuclear distributions. Using this dataset, we present a novel virtual staining framework that translates BIT volumes with shift-variant contrast into realistic H&E volumes by leveraging bidirectional multiscale content consistency and cross-domain style reuse to enhance structural fidelity and perceptual realism. Our method achieves state-of-the-art realism metrics while significantly improving 3D nuclei segmentation accuracy and boundary preservation under zero-shot Cellpose evaluation. Together, these contributions establish a quantitatively validated, structurally faithful, and scalable pipeline for 3D virtual H&E staining, advancing the paradigm of slide-free, volumetric computational histopathology. Our data and code are available at: https://github.com/aasong113/HistoBIT3D_VirtualStaining.

- 损失：Dice损失 + 边界感知正则项；该正则由分形维度的可微化近似构成，用于强化边界与形状保真。

Abstract: Biomedical image segmentation is a critical task in medical diagnosis and treatment planning, enabling precise delineation of anatomical structures and pathological regions. This paper introduces ConvNeXt-FD, a novel deep learning architecture for robust biomedical image segmentation, built upon a U-Net-like encoder-decoder framework leveraging the powerful ConvNeXt backbone. Our approach integrates a hybrid loss function combining the Dice coefficient with a boundary-aware regularization term inspired by a differentiable formulation of Fractal Dimension, designed to enhance the model's sensitivity to object boundaries and shape fidelity. The integration of ConvNeXt as a strong encoder, coupled with the boundary-aware regularization, proves effective in capturing both high-level semantic features and fine-grained boundary details, leading to more accurate and reliable segmentations in challenging biomedical contexts.

### [37] [Rethinking Token Reduction for Diffusion Models via Output-Similarity-Awareness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22011)
*Hangyeol Lee,Hyojeong Lee,Joo-Young Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DiTo：一种面向输出的扩散Transformer令牌裁剪范式。利用相邻时间步输出相似性稳定的观测，以“匹配步”建立令牌对应关系，并在后续“裁剪步”复用；通过PMR引导的区间调度决定匹配频率，并用频率感知匹配抑制重复复用造成的局部误差与块效应。实验显示在相当加速下较现有方法PSNR提升1.6–3.9 dB，获得更优帕累托前沿。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有令牌减少方法多沿用ViT的输入相似性假设，仅基于输入特征做聚合/裁剪，忽略扩散生成的最终目标是最小化重建误差，因而应关注输出令牌的相似性。这种“输入中心”的假设与生成任务目标存在错配，导致效率/质量权衡不理想。

Method: 1) 输出中心的令牌裁剪：观察到相邻扩散步中输出令牌相似性保持稳定；在“匹配步”用前一时刻的输出相似性作为代理，构建令牌对应与分组；2) 复用策略：将该对应关系在接下来的多个“裁剪步”中复用以减少计算；3) PMR（Pair Match Ratio）引导的区间调度：依据令牌对匹配率动态决定多长间隔再次执行匹配步，权衡开销与准确性；4) 频率感知匹配：对被高频复用的匹配增加惩罚，缓解局部近似误差累积与块状伪影。

Result: 在与现有TR方法相当的加速比下，PSNR提升1.6–3.9 dB；整体呈现更优的速度-质量帕累托前沿；有效降低块状伪影与误差累积。

Conclusion: 以输出相似性为核心的DiTo打破了基于输入相似性的传统TR范式，通过匹配-裁剪交替与PMR自适应调度、频率感知约束，实现显著更好的质量-效率权衡，为扩散Transformer的高效推理提供了通用思路。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) achieve superior image generation quality but suffer from quadratic computational complexity relative to token count. While various token reduction (TR) methods have been proposed to mitigate this cost, they overlook the primary objective of generative models: minimizing recovery error, which requires reflecting output token similarity. They rely solely on input token similarity inherited from reduction-only ViT paradigms, leading to a fundamental misalignment with this objective.
  To bridge this gap, we propose DiTo, a novel TR paradigm that shifts the focus toward output-centric token reduction. Based on the observation that output token similarity is consistently preserved across adjacent timesteps, DiTo utilizes prior-step similarities as an effective proxy to establish token correspondences at a Matching timestep, which are then reused across multiple subsequent Reduction timesteps. To optimize this interleaved scheduling, we propose Pair Match Ratio (PMR)-guided Interval Scheduling to determine the optimal matching frequency. Furthermore, to mitigate localized approximation errors and resulting blocking artifacts caused by repeated reuse, we propose Frequency-aware Token Matching by incorporating a selection-frequency penalty. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DiTo consistently outperforms existing TR methods with 1.6-3.9 dB higher PSNR at comparable speedups, achieving a superior Pareto frontier.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在生成式3D分类与描述任务上达到SOTA，同时在真实扫描点云与多轮对话场景中展现出强泛化与稳健性。

Conclusion: 数据驱动的CoT监督可以有效赋能3D点云多模态模型的显式推理与下游性能；通过高质量数据构建与HiLPO，可将CoT成功迁移至3D领域，形成性能与泛化双提升的PointLLM-R。

Abstract: Understanding 3D point clouds through language remains a fundamental challenge in computer graphics and visual computing, due to the irregular structure of point cloud data and the lack of explicit reasoning in existing 3D multimodal models. While Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning has shown strong effectiveness in LLMs and image-based MLLMs, its extension to 3D understanding remains largely underexplored. In this paper, we propose a data-centric framework for constructing large-scale CoT supervision tailored to 3D point cloud understanding. Our framework consists of a two-stage pipeline that first refines point-text instruction data via vision-language-model-based quality evaluation and reference-guided refinement, and then synthesizes high-quality reasoning paths through Human-in-the-Loop Prompt Optimization (HiLPO). Using this approach, we build PoCoTI, a CoT-enhanced point-text instruction-following dataset containing 55K samples with explicit reasoning paths. Fine-tuning PointLLM on PoCoTI yields PointLLM-R, a reasoning-capable 3D multimodal language model. Extensive experiments on generative 3D classification and captioning demonstrate that PointLLM-R achieves state-of-the-art performance and generalizes robustly to real-world scanned point clouds and multi-turn dialogue scenarios.

### [39] [ORBIS: Output-Guided Token Reduction with Distribution-Aware Matching for Video Diffusion Acceleration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22015)
*Hangyeol Lee,Joo-Young Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ORBiS：面向视频Diffusion Transformer的软硬协同加速器，利用上一步激活改进跨token相似度与匹配质量，引入分布感知匹配算法DATM，并以深度流水与量化隐藏/降低开销；在同精度下较SOTA提升约2倍token压缩、最高4.5×加速与79.3%能耗降低。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频DiT因3D时空注意力随帧数线性扩展导致算力和能耗骤增；现有token压缩方法依赖粗糙相似度估计与轻量匹配，匹配质量差、加速有限。需要更准确的相似度、更优的匹配算法及能被硬件高效实现的整体方案。

Method: 软硬协同：1) 利用上一个扩散时间步的输出激活估计更准确的跨token相似度，驱动更高质量的token合并/裁剪；2) 提出Distribution-Aware Token Matching（DATM），建模全局token分布并最小化显式token对损失，提升匹配鲁棒性与效果；3) 硬件方面设计专用深度流水化单元以完全隐藏DATM延迟，并通过量化降低面积与能耗，DATM相关逻辑仅占总面积2.4%，精度损失可忽略。

Result: 相较最新方法AsymRnR，ORBiS实现约2×更高的token削减比；与NVIDIA A100 GPU对比可获得最高4.5×速度提升与79.3%能耗降低；同时保持生成质量基本不变（精度损失可忽略）。

Conclusion: 通过利用时间步间信息与分布感知匹配，并以专用、量化、深度流水硬件实现，ORBiS显著提高视频DiT的token压缩与整体效率，在不显著牺牲质量的前提下实现大幅加速与能耗降低，优于现有SOTA。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformer (DiT) has emerged as a powerful model architecture for generating high-quality images and videos. In the case of video DiT, 3D Spatio-Temporal Attention increases token length in proportion to the number of frames, sharply increasing computational cost. Token reduction methods mitigate this cost by exploiting spatial redundancy, but existing approaches rely on inaccurate similarity estimates and lightweight matching algorithms, resulting in poor matching quality and only marginal acceleration.
  To overcome these limitations, we propose ORBIS, an SW-HW co-designed accelerator for video DiT. ORBIS leverages the output activation from the previous timestep to obtain more accurate inter-token similarity, substantially improving matching quality and enabling a higher token reduction ratio. We further introduce a Distribution-Aware Token Matching (DATM) algorithm that captures global token distribution and explicitly minimizes token-pair loss for additional gains. To fully hide DATM latency, we design specialized, deeply pipelined hardware and minimize its hardware cost through quantization, occupying only 2.4% of total area with negligible accuracy loss. Extensive experiments show that ORBIS achieves about 2x higher token reduction ratio than the state-of-the-art approach, AsymRnR, while delivering up to 4.5x speedup and 79.3% energy reduction compared to an NVIDIA A100 GPU.

This information is incorporated through a guidance mechanism to enhance the diversity and expressiveness of predicted motions. ### [42] [ForeSplat: Optimization-Aware Foresight for Feed-Forward 3D Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22020)
*Yuke Li,Weihang Liu,Cheng Zhang,Yuefeng Zhang,Jiadi Cui,Zixuan Wang,Junran Ding,Haoyu Wu,Yujiao Shi,Jingyi Yu,Xin Lou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ForeSplat是一种面向优化的训练框架，用于前馈式3D高斯点渲染（3DGS）：通过在训练中模拟少量后续优化步骤，并用轻量的多锚点一阶“元梯度”信号指导网络，使其预测结果成为极易被快速微调优化器改进的初始化。无需增加推理成本，少量 refinement 步即可在秒级达到更高质量，并在多种骨干（AnySplat、Pi3X、蒸馏小模型）上显著优于标准前馈3DGS。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前馈3DGS推理快但难以达到每场景优化（per-scene optimization）的上限，且缺乏大规模3D标注限制了单次预测的上限。现实折中是“先预测再精炼”，但现有前馈模型仅最小化零步渲染误差，未考虑其输出是否利于后续优化快速收敛。因此需要一种训练方式，让模型学会产出对下游优化器友好的初始化，从而以更小模型获得高保真重建。

Method: 提出ForeSplat：在训练阶段内嵌一个短内环的3DGS优化轨迹，沿轨迹采样若干“锚点”状态，以一阶梯度聚合形成替代的优化感知信号（MetaGrad），避免昂贵的高阶反传。将该信号反传至预测头，促使前馈网络输出对后续优化更可精炼的参数。该框架可用于多种骨干（AnySplat、Pi3X、蒸馏版），训练完成后推理成本不变，仅需少量refinement步即可快速逼近甚至超过完全收敛的基线。

Result: 在所有测试架构上，使用ForeSplat训练的初始化相比原始前馈3DGS：1) 需要更少的refinement步数即可达到高质量；2) 达到更高的峰值重建质量（即使与完全收敛的原始方法相比）；3) 小模型也能实现高保真重建，显著缩小摊销预测与按场景优化之间的性能差距。

Conclusion: 优化感知训练让前馈3DGS把部分建模负担交给后续优化器，实现“好初始化+快速精炼”的协同：不增推理成本、秒级达到高质量、适配多骨干并稳定超越基线，为轻量级高保真3D重建提供可行路径。

Abstract: Feed-forward 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) models offer fast single-pass reconstruction,but scaling them to match per-scene optimization quality is fundamentally hindered by the scarcity of large-scale 3D annotations.A practical compromise is predict-then-refine,where post-prediction optimization compensates for the limited capacity of the feed-forward network.However,standard feed-forward 3DGS is trained solely for zero-step rendering error,ignoring whether its output constitutes a good initialization for the downstream optimizer.We present ForeSplat,an optimization-aware training framework that equips feed-forward 3DGS models to produce initializations explicitly designed for rapid,effective refinement.By offloading part of the scene-modeling burden to the optimizer,ForeSplat substantially reduces the capacity pressure on the feed-forward model,making high-quality reconstruction feasible even with compact networks.At its core is MetaGrad,a lightweight multi-anchor meta-gradient training rule that bypasses costly higher-order differentiation through the 3DGS optimizer.MetaGrad unrolls a short inner-loop refinement trajectory,samples anchor states,and back-propagates aggregated first-order gradients to the prediction head as a surrogate optimization-aware signal.This fine-tuning adds no inference cost and enables high-quality reconstruction within seconds after a few refinement steps.We instantiate ForeSplat on diverse backbones,including AnySplat,Pi3X,and a distilled variant tailored for edge deployment.Across all tested architectures,a ForeSplat-trained initialization converges in fewer refinement steps and reaches a higher peak reconstruction quality than its vanilla counterpart,even fully converged.The framework consistently bridges the gap between amortized prediction and per-scene optimization,establishing a practical path toward lightweight,high-fidelity 3D reconstruction.

### [43] [SO-Mamba: State-Ownership Mamba for Unrolled MRI Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22031)
*Pengcheng Fang,Hongli Chen,Fangfang Tang,Feng Liu,Xiaohao Cai,Shanshan Shan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SO-Mamba，一种在迭代重建解耦“驻留/非驻留”证据的Mamba正则器，通过状态归属与路由提高长程一致性与细节恢复，在五个MRI基准上优于CNN/Transformer/Mamba基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 加速MRI需在保证大范围解剖一致性的同时恢复缺失细节。Mamba等状态空间模型具有效率高的长程建模能力，但在与数据一致性耦合的展开式重建中，各阶段处理的重建迭代不同：应有跨阶段持久的“驻留”信息载体，以及仅对当前更新有效的“非驻留”证据。若不加区分，二者会混入同一循环内容通道，导致状态污染与更新漂移。

Method: 提出SO-Mamba，在每个Mamba阶段为证据分配三种“所有权”：(1) 驻留载体进入循环内容通道；(2) 通过B/C接口的仿射调制进行状态接口访问；(3) 经输出校正通道进行非状态的增益修正。以State-Ownership Router (SOR)实现路由：构建驻留载体供Mamba内容路径循环，非驻留证据仅调制接口与输出，不进入循环内容。另提出两级“外带泄漏”诊断，将选择性扫描的隐藏状态轨迹与读出后的能量分离度量，以区分隐藏存储与读出表达。

Result: 在五个公开MRI重建基准（多解剖、多采样、多线圈）上，SO-Mamba在图像质量上持续优于CNN、Transformer与标准Mamba基线，同时保持竞争性的计算效率。

Conclusion: 区分驻留与非驻留证据并以SOR进行状态归属与路由，能避免循环路径被瞬时更新信息污染，强化跨阶段一致性与细节恢复；外带泄漏诊断为状态存储与读出解耦提供可测工具。SO-Mamba因此成为展开式MRI重建中高效、稳健的正则化模块。

Abstract: Accelerated MRI reconstruction requires recovering missing details while preserving anatomically coherent structures across large spatial regions. State-space models such as Mamba provide efficient long-range modeling, making them attractive learned regularizers for unrolled reconstruction. However, in a data-consistency-coupled unrolled solver, different stages operate on different reconstruction iterates, where the resident carrier should preserve coherent reconstruction content across stages while stage-dependent non-resident evidence is tied to the current update. Treating these roles uniformly can place persistent resident-carrier evidence and update-dependent non-resident evidence into the same recurrent content route. We therefore propose SO-Mamba, a state-ownership Mamba regularizer that assigns reconstruction evidence within each Mamba stage to recurrent residency, state-interface access, and non-state output correction. SO-Mamba implements this ownership rule with a State-Ownership Router (SOR), which constructs a resident carrier for recurrent content and routes non-resident evidence to affine modulation of the B/C state interfaces and an output correction outlet. The resident carrier supplies the Mamba content route, while the non-resident evidence stream adapts the state interfaces and contributes through the output outlet without entering the recurrent content route. We further introduce a two-level outer-band leakage diagnostic that separates hidden-state storage from readout expression by measuring outer-band energy in the selective-scan state trajectory and the post-scan Mamba readout. Experiments on five public MRI reconstruction benchmarks spanning diverse anatomies, sampling patterns, and coil configurations show that SO-Mamba consistently improves over CNN-, Transformer-, and Mamba-based baselines with competitive computational efficiency.

### [44] [AgroVG: A Large-Scale Multi-Source Benchmark for Agricultural Visual Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22034)
